2876<p>

2877Cabinets sit at the intersection of style and function, which is why choosing the right style, size, and color is so important. Theyre an instant focal point in bathrooms and kitchens, the foundation supporting the rest of the room. Our guide covers exactly what you need to know as you shop for cabinets for your home.&nbsp;</p>

2883<h2>

2884Whats the Best Cabinet Construction?</h2>

2885</div>

2886</div>

2887</div>

2888</div>

2889</div>

2890</div>

2891</div>

2892</div>

2893</div>

2894</div>

2895</div>

2896</div>

2897</div>

2898<div class="">

2899<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-bebcc-b-c-ada-cbc">

2934<p>

2935&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>

2936

2937

2938<h3>

2939Materials</h3>

2940

2941

2942<p>

2943There are several <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/cabinet-materials/" target="_blank">

2944common cabinet materials</a>

2945 you can use: particle board, medium density fiberboard (MDF), high density fiberboard (HDF), and plywood. All are forms of engineered wood, but their density and stability are different.</p>

2946

2947

2948<ul>

2949

2950 <li>

2951<strong>

2952Particle Board: </strong>

2953Made from small wood particles fused together with resin. This is the least dense and durable, but the most affordable. It&rsquo;s used primarily as an affordable option for cabinet boxes, but it tends to sag and buckle under heavy weights.&nbsp;</li>

2954

2955 <li>

2956<strong>

2957Plywood:</strong>

2958 Thinly sliced layers of wood are bonded together with resin and high-pressure. This is the strongest of the four, making it the best choice to use in cabinet boxes and frames.</li>

2959

2960 <li>

2961<strong>

2962MDF:</strong>

2963 Made from wood fibers instead of particles, MDF uses resins and high pressure to bond everything together. Works best for shelves and doors since it isn&rsquo;t as susceptible to warping as wood is.</li>

2964

2965 <li>

2966<strong>

2967HDF:</strong>

2968 Similar to MDF but denser and stronger. Works well for shelves or doors. HDF is also much more resistant to warping than wood, which is why it works so well for doors.</li>

2969

2970 <li>

2971<strong>

2972Solid Wood: </strong>

2973<a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/wood-kitchen-cabinet-types/" target="_blank">

2974Wood cabinets</a>

2975 features a beautiful wood grain that offers a natural look to any room. Because it is completely natural, it is susceptible to expanding and contracting over time. However, it&rsquo;s also a long-lasting material as well.</li>

2976

2977</ul>

2978

2979

2980<p>

2981All the Wilora cabinet boxes we sell are made from either &frac12;&rdquo; or &frac34;&rdquo; thick plywood for a more durable construction than is found with particle board.&nbsp;</p>

2982

2983

2984<p>

2985&nbsp;</p>

2986

2987

2988<h3>

2989Framed vs Frameless</h3>

2990

2991

2992<p>

2993Both framed and frameless cabinet styles each have their pros and cons. It all comes down to your personal preference.</p>

2994

2995

2996<p>

2997<strong>

2998Framed</strong>

2999</p>

3000

3001

3002<p>

3003These cabinets feature a frame installed to the front of the cabinet box. The drawers and doors are connected to the frame instead of the cabinet box. This frame serves as both a function and a style, as it adds durability and rigidity to the cabinet box &nbsp;while providing a classic look when you open a cabinet door.&nbsp;</p>

3004

3005

3006<p>

3007The main drawback with framed cabinets is access. &nbsp;Since the frame is 1&rdquo; to 2&rdquo; wider than the thickness of the cabinet box, the frame can get in the way when storing or retrieving things like pots, pans, or spices.&nbsp;</p>

3008

3009

3010<p>

3011With our framed selection of Wilora Hawthorne cabinets, the box interiors and exteriors are also given a UV coating to add protection to the natural Wood veneer finish.&nbsp;</p>

3012

3013

3014<p>

3015<strong>

3016Frameless</strong>

3017</p>

3018

3019

3020<p>

3021The doors of a frameless cabinet attach directly to the cabinet box, so there&rsquo;s no need for a front frame. Generally, a frameless cabinet is easier to utilize and access. On the other hand, it weakens the cabinet box, especially if you use subpar materials. This is why a frameless cabinet box needs to be thicker than a cabinet box used on a framed style.&nbsp;</p>

3022

3023

3024<p>

3025For this reason, our <a href="https://vevano.com/search/?q=wilora%20paloma&amp;utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

3026Wilora Paloma</a>

3027 selection of frameless cabinets feature &frac34;&rdquo; plywood boards in the construction of the cabinet boxes. The additional thickness provides the rigid stability necessary for holding doors and drawers. The Paloma collection also features European style flat-slab doors and drawers rather than the five-piece designs of our framed cabinet doors.</p>

3028

3029

3030<p>

3031&nbsp;</p>

3032

3033

3034<h3>

3035What&rsquo;s a Door Overlay? Why It Matters?</h3>

3036

3037

3038<p>

3039With framed cabinets, a door overlay refers to the exposed front frame.&nbsp;</p>

3040

3041

3042<ul>

3043

3044 <li>

3045With a <strong>

3046full overlay</strong>

3047, most of the frame is covered by the doors and drawers.&nbsp;</li>

3048

3049 <li>

3050With <strong>

3051partial overlay</strong>

3052, part of the frame is exposed.&nbsp;</li>

3053

3054 <li>

3055An <strong>

3056inset overlay</strong>

3057 occurs when the door is flush with the frame.&nbsp;</li>

3058

3059</ul>

3060

3061

3062<p>

3063Our selection of cabinets offers full overlay for a more beautiful appearance.</p>

3064

3065

3066<p>

3067&nbsp;</p>

3068

3069

3070<h2>

3071Which Cabinet Door Type Do You Like Best?</h2>

3072

3073

3074<p>

3075The door drives the style of your cabinets because this is what people see when they enter a room. With that in mind, there are three main styles of cabinet door and drawer: slab, shaker, and raised panel. There are other types, such as mullion and open-frame doors, but these are used sparingly. Most drawer and door designs fall into one of these three types. There&rsquo;s arguably no difference in quality of the different styles. The differences are purely aesthetic, so choose one that you love.</p>

3076

3116<h3>

3117<strong>

3118Slab</strong>

3119</h3>

3120

3121<p>

3122A slab style door is one solid piece and flat across the entire surface. Its primarily used with frameless cabinet boxes to provide a smooth, minimalist appearance. As a bonus, the flat surface is easy to clean and maintain. The slab door is often referred to as a European style, but it leans well into modern, contemporary, and industrial designs.&nbsp;</p>

3162<h3>

3163<strong>

3164Shaker</strong>

3165</h3>

3166

3167

3168<p>

3169The Shaker style door is named after its inventors, the Shakers, a religious group that split from the Quakers in the 1700s. Shakers were known for their skill in woodworking and carpentry, inventing a simple yet beautiful design we still use today. This timeless door style features five pieces, a recessed center panel framed by four raised pieces. This style is very flexible, working within transitional, classic, <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/cottage-style-decor-interior-design/" target="_blank">

3170cottage style</a>

3171, farmhouse, and contemporary looks.&nbsp;</p>

3212<h3>

3213<strong>

3214Raised Panel&nbsp;</strong>

3215</h3>

3216

3217<p>

3218A raised panel door features a contoured center panel tucked into a four-piece frame like a shaker door. But instead of a recessed panel, the beveled edges of the center panel create the appearance of a raised panel. Contouring ranges from simple to elaborate, making this style a popular choice. It works particularly well with traditional, classic, cottage, farmhouse, and transitional styles.&nbsp;</p>

3320<a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets-kitchen-base/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

3321<strong>

3322Base cabinets</strong>

3323</a>

3324 rest on your floor and support your countertops, sinks, faucets, and ranges. As such, it&rsquo;s important to pick the right configuration for your home.&nbsp;</p>

3325

3326

3327<p>

3328We offer many base cabinets, from the ultra-thin 6&rdquo; base cabinet to the 55&rdquo; blind corner base cabinet. With heights ranging from 27&rdquo; to 42&rdquo; and a depth ranging between 24&rdquo; and 32&rdquo;, you can find a size to fit your needs.&nbsp; &nbsp;</p>

3329

3330

3331<p>

3332Types include sink base cabinets with false drawers, dozens of drawer and door combos, cabinets made entirely of drawers, cabinets with full height doors, and more. Some base cabinets include customized cabinet organization hardware from Rev-A-Shelf, such roll-out drawers, trash bins, and more. We also carry specialty base cabinets, like our thin 6&rdquo; spice rack cabinet and corner cabinets with built-in Lazy Susans.&nbsp;</p>

3333

3334

3335<p>

3336Stick with one style for consistency or mix and match to fit your needs. There are no wrong choices. Only the right one for you.</p>

3344<strong>

3345Wall Cabinets</strong>

3346</p>

3347

3348

3349<p>

3350<a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets-kitchen-wall/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

3351Wall cabinets</a>

3352 install on the wall above base cabinets for storing glassware, bakeware, spices, utensils, and food. While the width and height range a lot, between 6&rdquo; and 40&rdquo;, these upper cabinets are typically half as deep as the base cabinets. As such, most of our wall cabinets are 12&rdquo; deep, but we include refrigerator wall cabinets as deep as 24&rdquo;.&nbsp;</p>

3353

3354

3355<p>

3356Types include one door, two door, and corner cabinet types. Door designs include slab, shaker, raised panel, open-frame glass*and flip-up to provide a better fit for your kitchen.</p>

3357

3358

3359<p>

3360*Glass not included. Due to fragility in shipping, the glass must be sourced locally.</p>

3369Tall Cabinets</strong>

3370</p>

3371

3372

3373<p>

3374<a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets-kitchen-tall/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

3375Tall cabinets</a>

3376, also known as pantry or utility cabinets, are like wall and base cabinets put together, plus a bit more. This type starts at the floor and reaches towards the ceiling to maximize storage space in the kitchen. While not as versatile as wall or base cabinets, there are quite a few configurations available.&nbsp;</p>

3377

3378

3379<p>

3380Choose from cabinets made completely of doors or drawers, or a combination of the two. Select a style with built-in space for wall ovens, whether you have one or two.</p>

3389Choose the Best Cabinets for Your Kitchen</strong>

3390</p>

3391

3392

3393<p>

3394With so many types and styles available, there are a wide assortment of design possibilities. Some prefer to use base cabinets on their own, preferring open shelving or a minimal look for the kitchen. Others may prefer the traditional approach of base cabinets and wall cabinets, while others may combine wall, base, and tall cabinets to create the ideal kitchen. That&rsquo;s the wonderful part of cabinets! Even with something so functional, you can shape it to your lifestyle. And with our wide range of ready-to-assemble cabinets, you get a customized kitchen without the customized price.</p>

3454Most bathroom cabinets are variations of base cabinets, since it&rsquo;s rare (though not unheard of) to hang a wall cabinet in a bathroom. These cabinets range from 12&rdquo; wide four-drawer variations to 60&rdquo; four-door sink base cabinets with six drawers and multiple false drawers.&nbsp;</p>

3455

3458When designing your vanity cabinets, consider who uses the bathroom and their habits. For example, a bathroom used by three people needs enough drawers to accommodate their pleasantries.</p>

3459

These are convenient, as the countertop doesn&rsquo;t attach to the wall, allowing you to move the freestanding cabinet like furniture. That said, buying your <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets-bathroom/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

3463bathroom cabinets</a>

3464 separate from your counter and sink allows for greater flexibility in customizing the look and feel of your bathroom.&nbsp;</p>

So whether you&rsquo;re looking to outfit a small guest bathroom or the master bath suite, we have the right bathroom cabinets for your home. Pair your new cabinet with the ideal sink and faucet for a personalized look you&rsquo;ll love. &nbsp;</p>

3496<h3>

3497Laundry Room Cabinets</h3>

3498

3499

3500<p>

3501Laundry room cabinets are just kitchen cabinets installed in a laundry room. As such, the style and variety isn&rsquo;t different, though some people choose simpler, more affordable cabinets since the laundry room is more about utility than style.&nbsp;</p>

3502

3503

3504<p>

3505Add <a href="https://vevano.com/search/?q=base%20cabinets&amp;utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

3506base cabinets</a>

3507 for an easy yet accessible space to store irons, ironing boards, or folded linens, while the countertop makes a great place to pretreat stains or fold clothing.&nbsp;</p>

3512Wall cabinets</a>

3513 look stunning above the washer and dryer, creating a perfect space to safely store bleach and detergents out of the way.&nbsp;</p>

3518Tall cabinets</a>

3519 provide optimized storage for sheets, bedding, towels, and other linens in one central location. The best part of installing cabinets in a laundry room is how clean and organized the room stays thanks to plentiful storage options. Goodbye clutter, hello clean.</p>

3530<p>

3531Cabinets, either base or wall styles, make an excellent addition to a home theater room or bar area. They provide a classy, inviting look with the promise of goodies and treats inside. 3532lighting</a>

3533 to add to the aesthetic of a room, even add a <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/flooring-tile-backsplash/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

3534backsplash</a>

3535 by the cabinets for complementary flair. Store beverages, snacks, and condiments in an easily accessible place that stays organized and declutters the room. For theater rooms, use cabinets to store movies, gaming systems, blankets, and board games for easy access.</p>

3542<h2>

3543Cabinet Heights and Sizes</h2>

3544

3545

3546<p>

3547We offer cabinets in a wide variety of sizes, allowing countless combinations so you can find the functionality of <a href="https://vevano.com/page/custom-kitchen-cabinet-collections/" target="_blank">

3548custom cabinets</a>

3549 without the high price tag. Cabinet widths start at 6&rdquo; with sizes spanning up to 60&rdquo;. For heights, there are even more options, starting 12&rdquo; and going up to 96&rdquo; high. Depths range from 12&rdquo; to 36&rdquo;. These sizes cover base, wall, and tall cabinets, as well as specialty cabinets like spice racks, wine racks, and more to maximize your available space.&nbsp;</p>

3556<h2>

3557Cabinet Features to Look For</h2>

3558

3559

3560<p>

3561Looks matter. But style means little if it&rsquo;s not functional. As you shop for the right cabinets for your home, there are some features to look for to optimize the functionality. Quality features help to extend the life of cabinetry and make your life easier (and quieter).</p>

3562

3563

3564<p>

3565&nbsp;</p>

3566

3567

3568<p>

3569<strong>

3570Drawer Slides</strong>

3571</p>

3572

3573

3574<p>

3575<a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/hardware-cabinets/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

3576Drawer slides</a>

3577 are located on the sides or under the drawer to help it move back and forth. Slides can either be install on the sides of the drawer, or underneath (called an under-mount slide). Premium cabinets use soft-close mechanism built into the slide so drawers don&rsquo;t slam as they shut. Even if you try to slam a drawer, the soft-close feature slows &nbsp;down to a smooth, soft stop.&nbsp;</p>

3578

3579

3580<p>

3581Another feature to look for is whether the slides are full extension or not. Full extension means the drawer can be fully extended to see everything within the drawer. A &frac34; extension glide leaves &frac14; of the drawer inaccessible, making it harder to access items in the back of the drawer. That&rsquo;s why full extension matters. It&rsquo;s a small thing, but it affects your drawer organization later.&nbsp;</p>

3582

3583

3584<p>

3585Our framed cabinets feature Blum undermount, full extension soft-close drawer slides, so the hardware stay out of sight yet remains functional.&nbsp;</p>

3586

3587

3588<p>

3589Our frameless cabinets feature Blum&rsquo;s &ldquo;LegraBox&rdquo; technology for a full extension, soft-close drawer as well.</p>

3590

3591

3592<p>

3593&nbsp;</p>

3594

3595

3596<p>

3597<strong>

3598Hinges</strong>

3599</p>

3600

3601

3602<p>

3603Even cabinet hinges are an indicator of quality. Much like drawers and drawer slides, a high-quality cabinet has soft-close hinges. These hinges prevent slamming doors, which extends the life of your cabinet boxes and doors alike. Quality hinges also make it easy to remove and re-attach doors for cleaning, painting, or organizing.</p>

3604

3605

3606<p>

3607Known for their excellence in crafting quality cabinet hardware and accessories, Blum is a premium brand of hinges (and drawer slides). All our Wilora Paloma and Wilora Hawthorne cabinets come with soft-close Blum hardware. No upgrades required.</p>

3608

3609

3610<p>

3611&nbsp;</p>

3612

3613

3614<p>

3615<strong>

3616Bumpers</strong>

3617</p>

3618

3619

3620<p>

3621A sign of a quality cabinet is if there are soft bumpers made of rubber on the inside corner of the cabinet door or drawer. These little pieces minimize the loud thud associated with shutting a door a bit too roughly. Over time, these may need to be replaced over the life of your cabinets, which is easy to do, especially if you choose the self-adhesive kind.</p>

3622

3623

3987

3988

3989<h2>

3990Tantalizing Two-Tone Cabinets&nbsp;</h2>

3991

3992

3993<p>

3994A practice that&rsquo;s quickly catching on is using two colors of cabinets. There are a couple ways to do this to make sure colors work well in tandem.&nbsp;</p>

3995

3996

3997<p>

3998The most common method is to choose one color for the base cabinets and one for the wall cabinets. A general rule is to keep the base cabinets a darker color than the wall cabinets. Placing the darker color, such as dark grey, on the floor anchors the room, while the lighter color, perhaps a light grey, opens it up to create balance between the two.&nbsp;</p>

3999

4000

4001<p>

4002Another method is to choose a color for the kitchen island while the base, wall, and tall cabinets are a different color or shade. This provides an additional pop of dimension to the room, preventing it from potentially looking flat.</p>

4003

4004

4005<p>

4006&nbsp;</p>

4007

4008

4009<h2>

4010Cabinet Finish: Paint, Stain, or Glaze&nbsp;</h2>

4011

4012

4013<p>

4014There are three options for cabinet finishes: paint, stain, or glaze. Each one has different properties and strengths that affect the longevity and appearance of your cabinets. The look also depends on the material of your cabinet doors. MDF and HDF don&rsquo;t have wood grain, so they can&rsquo;t be stained like solid wood.&nbsp;</p>

4015

4016

4017<p>

4018&nbsp;</p>

4019

4020

4021<p>

4022<strong>

4023Painted Cabinets</strong>

4024</p>

4025

4026

4027<p>

4028Painted cabinets feature an &nbsp;even coat, providing an opaque layer of solid color, hiding any wood grains or defining markings. Because of its smooth, pure appearance, it works best on MDF or HDF doors. On wood doors, paint hides the wood grain below, which may be a positive or negative depending on how you feel about wood grain.&nbsp;</p>

4029

4030

4031<p>

4032Paint is the best choice for a flawlessly smooth color and surface. The main drawback to paint is tends to peel and crack over time, so take that into consideration as you think about what&rsquo;s best for your home.&nbsp;</p>

4033

4034

4035<p>

4036&nbsp;</p>

4037

4038

4039<p>

4040<strong>

4041Stained Cabinets</strong>

4042</p>

4043

4044

4045<p>

4046Stains are a translucent coating meant to enhance the grain and natural features of wood. Where paint covers, stains seep into the grain itself, darkening features like grains and knots while adding rich color tones.&nbsp;</p>

4047

4048

4049<p>

4050Since it&rsquo;s translucent, stains are really only used with natural wood doors and cabinets instead of MDF or HDF materials, as these lack the natural grain stains are meant to enhance.&nbsp;</p>

4051

4052

4053<p>

4054Stained cabinets tend to be easier to maintain over time and last longer because it doesn&rsquo;t peel or crack. But stains don&rsquo;t have as many color options as paint, and they don&rsquo;t have the smoothness paint&rsquo;s consistency offers.</p>

4055

4056

4057<p>

4058&nbsp;</p>

4059

4060

4061<p>

4062<strong>

4063Glazed Cabinets</strong>

4064</p>

4065

4066

4067<p>

4068Glaze is applied over stains or paints to add more dimension and contrast to cabinets, particularly with shaker and raised-panel style doors. Where stains seep into the surface, glaze sits on top, with two different application methods that each have different effects.&nbsp;</p>

4069

4070

4071<p>

4072The first method is an accent glaze, which applies the glaze in corners and lines to create decorative contrast, like with our <a href="https://vevano.com/page/cabinets-white-wilora-hawthorne-shaker-antique-base/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4073antique white </a>

4074collection. It&rsquo;s used to highlight details in the cabinets without affecting the overall look. The second method is to add texture to the overall look of paints or stains.</p>

4075

4076

4077<p>

4078&nbsp;</p>

4079

4080

4081<p>

4082<strong>

4083Overall: Choose the Option You Love</strong>

4084</p>

4085

4086

4087<p>

4088Since paints and stains have such different qualities, it&rsquo;s best to choose the style you like over the style you think others like. Go with the perfectly smooth finish of paint or embrace the natural features stains enhance. We offer both types so you can find the best fit for your home.</p>

4089

4090

4091<p>

4092&nbsp;</p>

4228<div>

4229<p>

4230First hitting the art scene over a century ago, modern design &nbsp;focuses on clean lines with minimal decorative elements. Turning away from the unnecessary decorative details popular in the Victorian era, modern styles developed to elevate unobtrusive shapes and minimalism by focusing on function over form. As such, every element of the modern kitchen serves a purpose that&rsquo;s relaxing yet stylish.&nbsp;</p>

4231

4232

4233<p>

4234Cabinets are the anchor in defining a modern kitchen, so choice and color are important. For the optimal clean look, glossy white slab style cabinets are an ideal choice. White matches everything, offering a simple, uncomplicated look. To add a touch of color or wood tone, check out slab doors in colors like <a href="https://vevano.com/page/cabinets-gray-wilora-paloma-marquis-gray-wood-base/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4235grey wood</a>

4236, <a href="https://vevano.com/page/cabinets-white-wilora-paloma-marquis-white-pine-base/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4237white pine</a>

4238, <a href="https://vevano.com/page/cabinets-white-wilora-paloma-cortina-oyster-shell-base/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4239oyster shell</a>

4240, or <a href="https://vevano.com/page/cabinets-dark-wilora-paloma-marquis-dark-wood-base/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4241dark wood</a>

4242. Hues range from light and airy to dark and rich, matching your ideal aesthetic.</p>

4243

4244

4245<p>

4246When choosing pulls and knobs for&nbsp;<a href="https://vevano.com/page/modern-kitchen-cabinets/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4247modern kitchen cabinets</a>

4248, look for simple shapes with straight lines, smooth curves and very little beveling or other decorative details. Avoid pulls and knobs with floral patterns, excessive beveling, or knotwork designs. Popular finishes include glass, natural stone, wood, and chrome. This creates an inviting mixture of both manmade and organic elements to keep the room pleasing but inviting.</p>

The goal is to look beautiful, warm, and welcoming. Shaker cabinets or doors with raised panels work best with a classic look, with colors ranging from <a href="https://vevano.com/page/cabinets-white-wilora-hawthorne-wildwood-antique-white-base/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4313saddle</a>

4314. Additional accessories such as fluted legs, wine racks, and crown molding are classic flourishes for adding an upscale look to your cabinets.&nbsp;</p>

4377<p>

4378Transitional refers to a newer style that combines the sleek look of modern with a few decorative twists from traditional. It&rsquo;s bold and comfortable. And the best characteristic of transitional design is how well it lends itself to personalization and customization. While many interior design styles have well-defined rules, a transitional style is a hybrid. You choose what you want it to be.&nbsp;</p>

4379

4380

4381<p>

4382For cabinets, grey is popular because neutral tones match well with other finishes and accents. Both raised panel and shaker cabinet styles are popular in <a href="https://vevano.com/page/transitional-kitchen-cabinets/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4383transitional kitchens</a>

4384, and because it&rsquo;s such a flexible style it embraces a wide range of colors from light to dark and wood grains.</p>

4385

4386

4387<p>

4388With lighting fixtures, hardware, and faucets, stylish finishes include glass, polished nickel, gold, and matte black.&nbsp;</p>

4447<p>

4448<a href="https://vevano.com/page/industrial-kitchen-cabinets/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4449Industrial style kitchens</a>

4450 draw inspiration from manufacturing and industrial buildings. Transforming old factories and buildings into livable spaces holds an unexpected charm. Designing interiors featuring exposed brick, ductwork, plaster, cast-iron fixtures, and concrete is very popular, especially with the environmentally conscious.</p>

4451

4452

4453<p>

4454Industrial styles embrace raw minimalism, finding the beauty in bare architecture and utilizing it as an aesthetic feature rather than a blemish to cover up. When selecting the right cabinets for an industrial look, a flat slab door provides a minimalist aesthetic that works well, or shaker doors are a simple option that add dimension.. White and grey are popular because neutrals match everything, while wood tones pair well with concrete or brick.</p>

4455

4456

4457<p>

4458For hardware, matte black, raw steel, oil-rubbed bronze, or polished nickel are popular finishes, especially when used with bar pull handles. Glass light fixtures featuring vintage Edison style bulbs are also a hallmark of this design. Choose a bright accent color such as red, blue, yellow, or green to catch the eye.</p>

4516<div>

4517<p>

4518<a href="https://vevano.com/page/cottage-kitchen-cabinets/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4519Cottage kitchens</a>

4520 focus on light, airy spaces with touches of rustic simplicity. A few vintage elements, like an oil lantern and a white cast-iron sink, add old-fashioned charm, while linen window treatments and flannel tablecloths provide warmth. The cottage style is a blend of the old and new. It feels natural and inviting.&nbsp;</p>

4521

4522

4523<p>

4524With cottage style cabinets, antique white is the ideal color, with door styles varying between raised panel and Shaker. Glass doors both work well in this aesthetic, especially if you have fine china to show off. And accessories like fluted legs and wine racks add tasteful hints of refinement.</p>

4525

4526

4527<p>

4528Ornately decorative hardware works well with cottage cabinets, especially antique pewter, bronze, or iron. Consider latches for cabinets. These add an antique touch while keeping doors secure. Pair with wood floors or subway tiles to complete the look.</p>

4534

4535<h2>

4536Installing Your Kitchen Cabinets</h2>

4537

4538

4539<p>

4540When you purchase cabinets, you are either buying them custom made by a local woodworker, preassembled, or ready-to-assembled (RTA). Custom cabinets are expensive and time consuming to install. Preassembled cabinets require little work, as you simply mount the boxes and install the doors, but they have the highest risk of damage during the shipping process. &nbsp;RTA cabinets have the least risk of damage during shipping and are more affordable overall. &nbsp;</p>

4541

4542

4543<p>

4544For RTA cabinets, you have a couple options when assembling and installing your cabinets. You can choose to build and install them yourself or hire a professional. For the DIYer, check out our &nbsp;guide on how to install cabinets in your home..&nbsp;</p>

4545

4546

4547<p>

4548When we create a design of your cabinets, we annotate measurements to promote a smooth assembly and install experience. We also keep our installation instructions simple at less than three pages. Don&rsquo;t forget to download our instructions.&nbsp;</p>

4549

4727<h3>

4728Cabinet Accessories, Panels, Trims, and Additions</h3>

4729

4730

4731<p>

4732Adding accessories like trim and molding elevates the style of your cabinets while panels are necessary to complete the look. <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets-kitchen-parts-and-accessories/?filter=type_uFilter%3A%22Leg%22&amp;utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4733Legs</a>

4734 and <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets-kitchen-parts-and-accessories/?filter=type_uFilter%3A%22Foot%22&amp;utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4735feet</a>

4736 are popular decorative accessories you can pair with a pullout spice rack to be both functional and beautiful. <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets-kitchen-parts-and-accessories/?filter=type_uFilter%3A%22Corbel%22&amp;utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4737Corbels</a>

4738 are like brackets installed on range hoods or under cabinets for added support or decoration. These accessories range from simple to elaborate carved designs, meaning they&rsquo;re compatible with most styles.&nbsp;</p>

4739

4740

4741<p>

4742&nbsp;</p>

4743

4744

4745<p>

4746<strong>

4747Panels</strong>

4748</p>

4749

4750

4751<p>

4752<a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets-kitchen-parts-and-accessories/?filter=type_uFilter%3A%22Panel%22&amp;utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4753Panels</a>

4754 finish the look of your cabinets. If there is an exposed side of a cabinet box or an appliance you want to hide, there are panels to cover it, creating a consistent look throughout your kitchen. Toe kicks bridge the gap between the cabinet and the floor, covering up the cabinet legs. <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets-kitchen-parts-and-accessories/?filter=type_uFilter%3A%22Filler%22&amp;utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4755Fillers</a>

4756 cover any gaps between cabinets and appliances. <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets-kitchen-parts-and-accessories/?filter=type_uFilter%3A%22Valance%22&amp;utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4757Valances</a>

4758 add a decorative panel to bridge gaps between cabinets and ceilings or to decorate range hoods.&nbsp;</p>

4759

4760

4761<p>

4762&nbsp;</p>

4763

4764

4765<p>

4766<strong>

4767Molding</strong>

4768</p>

4769

4770

4771<p>

4772<a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets-kitchen-parts-and-accessories/?filter=type_uFilter%3A%22Molding%22&amp;utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4773Molding</a>

4774 is available for both above and below cabinetry. Crown molding sits atop the cabinets, adding a high-class look that goes perfectly with classic, cottage, and farmhouse styles. Toe-kick apron molding goes at the bottom. Rope molding features a curved design like the pattern of a rope. It works well as a decorative touch above or below cabinets and pairs with crown molding for a sophisticated look. Light rail molding is most often installed below wall cabinets to conceal under cabinet lighting while adding a classy touch.</p>

4775

4776

4777<p>

4778&nbsp;</p>

4779

4780

4781<p>

4782<strong>

4783Cabinet Touch Up Kits</strong>

4784</p>

4785

4786

4787<p>

4788<a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets-kitchen-parts-and-accessories/?filter=type_uFilter%3A%22Touch%20Up%20Kit%22&amp;utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4789Touch up kits</a>

4790 are small pen-like items that match the color of your cabinets. Hopefully you never actually need one, but if if your cabinets are scuffed or scratched, the touch-up kit is an easy way to fix the area. It is helpful to know you have a way to help repair it with a color that perfectly matches.</p>

4799

4800</div>

4801</div>

4802</div>

4803</div>

4804</div>

4805</div>

4814<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-cc-db--aeeb-dfd">

4816<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

4817<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

4818<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

4819<div class="">

4820<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-a-fb-d-ef-ffe">

4821<div class="merce-column-container">

4822<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-bfaeec-fd-a-f-edebdd">

4823<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf bfaeec-fd-a-f-edebdd-singleImageAlignment">

4824<img class="bfaeec-fd-a-f-edebdd-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/01M2qky23_fY4r7r6YU-i4YVWCy15zIdQwbCYe7zml8/rs:fill:840:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL0Jsb2clMjBQb3N0cy9VbHRpbWF0ZSUyMEd1aWRlJTIwdG8lMjBDYWJpbmV0cy9UaHVtYl9Eb29yUmVwbGFjZW1lbnRzLW1pbi5qcGc" alt="Drawer Hardware" title="Drawer Hardware"/>

4837<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-fa-b-cc-bf-bafe">

4838<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-fa-b-cc-bf-bafe">

4839<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

4840<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

4841<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

4842<div class="">

4843<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-caeb-e-da--dbffeeb">

4844<div class="merce-column-container">

4846<div>

4847<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4848<div>

4849<p>

4850Cabinet hardware includes pulls, knobs, and latches. Think of them like a watch on your wrist &ndash; functional yet beautiful. Hardware adds the final punctuation to the statement your cabinets make.&nbsp;</p>

4851

4852

4853<p>

4854<a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/hardware-cabinet-pulls/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4855Pulls</a>

4856 tend to be longer and bigger than knobs. Since your hand wraps around the pull, it provides greater leverage for opening and closing, making it ideal for drawers with heavy items and large doors. Lengths vary from around 1&rdquo; to over 30&rdquo;, meaning you have plenty of options for your cabinets, drawers and appliances. Consider the projection measurements, which tells you how far the pull protrudes from the cabinet. A longer projection allows for bigger hands and saves your knuckles from rubbing against cabinets. Projections range between &frac12;&quot; to 2&rdquo;. Popular shapes include cup handles, bar pulls, rectangular, and curved.&nbsp;</p>

4857

4858

4859<p>

4860<a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/hardware-cabinet-knobs/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4861Knobs</a>

4862 are smaller and designed for fingertips rather than palms. &nbsp;Shapes for knobs consist of square, rectangular, round, simple, detailed, beveled, artisanal, and even translucent styles. Knobs have projections ranging from &frac12;&quot; to 1 &frac34;&quot;, though it&rsquo;s not as important as a pull&rsquo;s projections.&nbsp;</p>

4863

4864

4865<p>

4866<a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/hardware-cabinets/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4867Latches</a>

4868 are a quick way to secure loose doors while adding a rustic touch. They&rsquo;re perfect for cottage and farmhouse kitchens. Latch styles range from simple to ornate, with materials like solid brass, stainless steel, nickel, gold, chrome, bronze, antiqued finishes, transparent acrylic, and matte black.</p>

4869

4870

4871<p>

4872&nbsp;</p>

4874

4875<h2>

4876How to Update Kitchen Cabinets Without Replacing Them</h2>

4877

4878

4879<p>

4880If new cabinets aren&rsquo;t a feasible option yet, you can take some steps to revitalize and extend the life of your current cabinets.&nbsp;</p>

4881

4882

4883<p>

4884&nbsp;</p>

4885

4886

4887<p>

4888<strong>

4889Replace or Add Parts</strong>

4890</p>

4891

4892

4893<p>

4894As glides and hinges get older, smooth motions becomes squeaky, rough, or parts may break altogether. Upgrade old hinges and slides with new versions to restore effortless motion and operation. If you&rsquo;re tired of being woken up on Saturday mornings from cabinet doors being slammed, add bumpers to the corners to dampen sounds and prevent banging and upgrade to soft-close hinges.</p>

4895

4896

4897<p>

4898&nbsp;</p>

4899

4900

4901<p>

4902<strong>

4903Add or Update Hardware</strong>

4904</p>

4905

4906

4907<p>

4908Cabinet pulls and knobs are an affordable way to upgrade the look and feel of your cabinets without having to redesign the entire room. Styles range from modern to vintage, from simple to ornate. Try a different finish. Change from knobs to pulls. Try a completely different design style for a new aesthetic.&nbsp;</p>

4909

4910

4911<p>

4912Older cabinets often don&rsquo;t stay closed when you shut them. To solve this problem, add a beautiful finish by installing latches to keep cabinets secure so they don&rsquo;t awkwardly hang open. These work well on wall, base, and tall cabinets.</p>

4913

4914

4915<p>

4916&nbsp;</p>

4917

4918

4919<p>

4920<strong>

4921Replace the Face</strong>

4922</p>

4923

4924

4925<p>

4926If your cabinet boxes are in good condition, you don&rsquo;t need to replace everything. In this case, you can change the face of the cabinets by choosing a different door style or color with our <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

4927replacement doors</a>

4928.&nbsp;</p>

4929

4930

4931<p>

4932Available in laminate, MDF, HDF, or solid birch, we carry doors and drawer fronts for both framed and frameless cabinet boxes. Choose a similar color to your boxes or add a different color for contrast.&nbsp;</p>

4933

4934

4935<p>

4936&nbsp;</p>

4948&nbsp;</p>

4949

4950

4951<h2>

4952Cabinet Design and Room Planning at Your Fingertips</h2>

4953

4954

4955<p>

4956While new cabinets are fantastic for reshaping the look of a room, you might find yourself overwhelmed at all the combinations, accessories, and styles. But what if you could have a personalized design from an expert? You <em>

4957can</em>

4958.&nbsp;</p>

4959

4960

4961<p>

4962Our designers are experts at turning &ldquo;I wish I could&hellip;&rdquo; into &ldquo;I&rsquo;m glad I did.&rdquo; Each room has potential. So, whether you have a small kitchen, a large one, a bathroom with uncommon measurements, or you want to transform a bedroom into something new,you have a professional dedicated to taking your vision to the next level.&nbsp;</p>

4963

4964

4965<p>

4966&nbsp;</p>

4967

4968

4969<h3>

4970Find Inspiration</h3>

4971

4972

4973<p>

4974We welcome your inspiration, whether from Pinterest, pictures of a loved one&rsquo;s remodel, a magazine, or a unique idea. We want to know everything so we can set to creating the ideal design for you, tailored to your taste and how you use the space.&nbsp;</p>

4975

4976

4977<p>

4978Share your favorite colors, finishes, fabrics, the kind of appliances or furniture you like. Every detail helps to inspire a design for your home.</p>

4979

4980

4981<p>

4982If you aren&rsquo;t sure what you like, we can help with that as well. That&rsquo;s one of the benefits of having your own personal designer.</p>

4983

4984

4985<p>

4986&nbsp;</p>

4987

4988

4989<h3>

4990Enjoy Personalized Design Services</h3>

4991

4992</div>

4993</div>

4994</div>

4995</div>

5016<img class="bcdc-e-a-bac-ddcfedd-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/Eq3-Tv64lYG8RrTGdEuD1PWKYz7QSf999eXbGrcFFdo/rs:fill:840:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL0Jsb2clMjBQb3N0cy9VbHRpbWF0ZSUyMEd1aWRlJTIwdG8lMjBDYWJpbmV0cy9Nb29kQm9hcmQtbWluLmpwZw" alt="Mood Board" title="Mood Board"/>

5040<div>

5041<p>

5042What does a designer actually <em>

5043do</em>

5044 for you? It&rsquo;s not just color palettes and d&eacute;cor. A designer takes all those details that make your home uniquely yours to create a rendering of what your real home could like - the shape of your room, where cabinets are currently located, what your lifestyle is like, whether you have kids or pets, where the plumbing is, and your inspiration. They&rsquo;ll tell you what floor matches the cabinets best, what kind of molding and details would bring out the aesthetic you&rsquo;re looking for, and what cabinet or&nbsp;<a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/kitchen-layout-ideas/" target="_blank">

5045kitchen layout</a>

5046 would make your life easiest.</p>

5047

5048

5049<p>

5050They don&rsquo;t stop there, either. Our designers take feedback from you to improve upon the design until you&rsquo;re satisfied. From there we keep your design as well as all of the products used on file so you can order when you&rsquo;re ready.</p>

5051

5052

5053<p>

5054&nbsp;</p>

5055

5056

5057<h3>

5058Sample Kits Delivered to Your Home</h3>

5059

5060

5061<p>

5062While a 3D rendering is great it&rsquo;s even better paired with samples. That&rsquo;s why we send a&nbsp;sample kit to your door. Compare the samples with your 3D rendering to test how everything looks under different lighting throughout the day and night. Compare how the different colors and materials look next to each other. Examine the quality of the cabinet door, the feel of the floor, the texture of the backsplash, how the samples work together to create a cohesive, refined palette to elevate the look of the room.</p>

5063

5064

5065<p>

5066&nbsp;</p>

5067

5068

5069<h2>

5070Cabinet FAQ</h2>

5071

5072

5073<p>

5074Below are some common questions about cabinets. If you have more questions that we haven&rsquo;t answered, feel free to ask us at <a href="mailto:design@vevano.com">

5075design@vevano.com</a>

5076.&nbsp;</p>

5077

5078

5079<p>

5080&nbsp;</p>

5081

5082

5083<p>

5084<strong>

5085What are RTA cabinets?</strong>

5086</p>

5087

5088

5089<p>

5090RTA stands for ready-to-assemble. These cabinets are shipped unassembled, or flat packed, to your home. You can assemble and install them or hire a professional.</p>

5091

5092

5093<p>

5094&nbsp;</p>

5095

5096

5097<p>

5098<strong>

5099How to Choose Hardware for Cabinets?</strong>

5100</p>

5101

5102

5103<p>

5104The first decision is to choose pulls or knobs. Both serve the same function, but some prefer handles to knobs, while others prefer knobs. You can also mix knobs and pulls for a more diverse look to your cabinets.</p>

5105

5106

5107<p>

5108Next, decide the finish. Contrasting finishes like chrome, brass, stainless steel, or polished nickel tend to work well on darker cabinets. For light colored cabinets you have a wider variety as both light-colored materials and contrasting tones work well.</p>

5109

5110

5111<p>

5112&nbsp;</p>

5113

5114

5115<p>

5116<strong>

5117How are wall cabinets attached to a wall?</strong>

5118</p>

5119

5120

5121<p>

5122With wall cabinets, a wooden support rail is attached the wall. Cabinets are then mounted to the wall &nbsp;where the studs are located. For more information on how cabinets are installed, see our cabinet install guide.</p>

5123

5124

5125<p>

5126&nbsp;</p>

5127

5128

5129<p>

5130<strong>

5131How do I design my cabinets?</strong>

5132</p>

5133

5134

5135<p>

5136You have a few options when designing your cabinets. You can shop and choose cabinets for your home according to what you need, using an interior design program to help you visualize the cabinets, but these programs require powerful computers and a moderate level of technical expertise. You can also go with a professional designer by hiring one in your area or go with one of Vevano&rsquo;s virtual&nbsp;interior designers. Our designers have years of experience in designing both new builds and remodels.</p>

5137

5138

5139<p>

5140&nbsp;</p>

5141

5142

5143<p>

5144<strong>

5145Can I paint my kitchen cabinets?</strong>

5146</p>

5147

5148

5149<p>

5150While you can paint your kitchen cabinets, we do recommend opting for a professional application, or buying newly painted kitchen cabinets that arrive the exact shade that you want. Professional painters ensure a smooth process and clean finish that lasts longer than most at-home applications. The same is true of new painted cabinets as well.</p>

5151

5152

5153<p>

5154&nbsp;</p>

5155

5156

5157<p>

5158<strong>

5159How much are kitchen cabinets?&nbsp;</strong>

5160</p>

5161

5162

5163<p>

5164Kitchen cabinet costs vary by style, customizations, and color, but a good rule of thumb is that, for in-stock cabinets, you can expect to pay $100 to $300 per linear foot. For more details on cabinet costs, check out our article <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/how-much-do-kitchen-cabinets-cost/">

5165&ldquo;How Much Do Kitchen Cabinets Cost?&rdquo;</a>

5166</p>

5167

5168

5169<p>

5170&nbsp;</p>

5171

5172

5173<p>

5174<strong>

5175How to measure kitchen cabinets?</strong>

5176</p>

5177

5178

5179<p>

5180To begin measuring your kitchen cabinets, start by drawing an outline of your kitchen. Mark any doors and windows you have. Next, mark where your cabinets and appliances are (or where you want them to be).&nbsp;</p>

5181

5182

5183<p>

5184Then start measuring the following:</p>

5185

5186

5187<ul>

5188

5189 <li>

5190Cabinet heights</li>

5191

5192 <li>

5193Lengths</li>

5194

5195 <li>

5196Depths</li>

5197

5198 <li>

5199Widths</li>

5200

5201 <li>

5202Distance between wall cabinets and base cabinets.&nbsp;</li>

5203

5204</ul>

5205

5206

5207<p>

5208For more detailed instructions and an example of what completed measurements might look like, see our post on <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/8-easy-steps-measuring-cabinets/">

5209&ldquo;8 Easy Steps for Measuring Your Kitchen for New Cabinets&rdquo;</a>

5210.</p>

5211

5212

5213<p>

5214&nbsp;</p>

5215

5216

5217<h2>

5218Ready to Find Your New Cabinets?</h2>

5219

5220

5221<p>

5222Now that you&rsquo;ve learned about the different styles, types, and sizes of cabinets, browse our <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

5223cabinet collection</a>

5224 to find the styles that match your home&rsquo;s aesthetic. If you&rsquo;d like to consult with one of our expert&nbsp;designers, check out our <a href="https://design.vevano.com/design-services/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide">

5225Design Services</a>

5226 page to get started. No measurements required. All we need to begin is your name, a contact method, and an image of your room to be redesigned.</p>

(MDF), high density fiberboard (HDF), and plywood. All are forms of engineered wood, but their density and stability are different.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cul\u003e\n\t\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eParticle Board: \u003c/strong\u003eMade from small wood particles fused together with resin. Works best for shelves and doors since it isn\u0026rsquo;t as susceptible to warping as wood is.\u003c/li\u003e\n\t\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eHDF:\u003c/strong\u003e Similar to MDF but denser and stronger. Works well for shelves or doors. HDF is also much more resistant to warping than wood, which is why it works so well for doors.\u003c/li\u003e\n\t\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSolid Wood: \u003c/strong\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/resource-center/wood-kitchen-cabinet-types/\" target=\"_blank\"\u003eWood cabinets\u003c/a\u003e features a beautiful wood grain that offers a natural look to any room. The drawers and doors are connected to the frame instead of the cabinet box. Generally, a frameless cabinet is easier to utilize and access. On the other hand, it weakens the cabinet box, especially if you use subpar materials. Most drawer and door designs fall into one of these three types. There\u0026rsquo;s arguably no difference in quality of the different styles. But style means little if it\u0026rsquo;s not functional. As you shop for the right cabinets for your home, there are some features to look for to optimize the functionality. Slides can either be install on the sides of the drawer, or underneath (called an under-mount slide). Premium cabinets use soft-close mechanism built into the slide so drawers don\u0026rsquo;t slam as they shut. Even if you try to slam a drawer, the soft-close feature slows \u0026nbsp;down to a smooth, soft stop.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eAnother feature to look for is whether the slides are full extension or not. Full extension means the drawer can be fully extended to see everything within the drawer. A \u0026frac34; extension glide leaves \u0026frac14; of the drawer inaccessible, making it harder to access items in the back of the drawer. That\u0026rsquo;s why full extension matters. It\u0026rsquo;s a small thing, but it affects your drawer organization later.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eOur framed cabinets feature Blum undermount, full extension soft-close drawer slides, so the hardware stay out of sight yet remains functional.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eOur frameless cabinets feature Blum\u0026rsquo;s \u0026ldquo;LegraBox\u0026rdquo; technology for a full extension, soft-close drawer as well.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eHinges\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eEven cabinet hinges are an indicator of quality. Much like drawers and drawer slides, a high-quality cabinet has soft-close hinges. These hinges prevent slamming doors, which extends the life of your cabinet boxes and doors alike. Quality hinges also make it easy to remove and re-attach doors for cleaning, painting, or organizing.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eKnown for their excellence in crafting quality cabinet hardware and accessories, Blum is a premium brand of hinges (and drawer slides). There are a couple ways to do this to make sure colors work well in tandem.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThe most common method is to choose one color for the base cabinets and one for the wall cabinets. A general rule is to keep the base cabinets a darker color than the wall cabinets. Placing the darker color, such as dark grey, on the floor anchors the room, while the lighter color, perhaps a light grey, opens it up to create balance between the two.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eAnother method is to choose a color for the kitchen island while the base, wall, and tall cabinets are a different color or shade. This provides an additional pop of dimension to the room, preventing it from potentially looking flat.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003eCabinet Finish: Paint, Stain, or Glaze\u0026nbsp;\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThere are three options for cabinet finishes: paint, stain, or glaze. Each one has different properties and strengths that affect the longevity and appearance of your cabinets. The look also depends on the material of your cabinet doors. MDF and HDF don\u0026rsquo;t have wood grain, so they can\u0026rsquo;t be stained like solid wood.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePainted Cabinets\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003ePainted cabinets feature an \u0026nbsp;even coat, providing an opaque layer of solid color, hiding any wood grains or defining markings. Because of its smooth, pure appearance, it works best on MDF or HDF doors. On wood doors, paint hides the wood grain below, which may be a positive or negative depending on how you feel about wood grain.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003ePaint is the best choice for a flawlessly smooth color and surface. The main drawback to paint is tends to peel and crack over time, so take that into consideration as you think about what\u0026rsquo;s best for your home.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eStained Cabinets\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eStains are a translucent coating meant to enhance the grain and natural features of wood. Where paint covers, stains seep into the grain itself, darkening features like grains and knots while adding rich color tones.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eSince it\u0026rsquo;s translucent, stains are really only used with natural wood doors and cabinets instead of MDF or HDF materials, as these lack the natural grain stains are meant to enhance.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eStained cabinets tend to be easier to maintain over time and last longer because it doesn\u0026rsquo;t peel or crack. But stains don\u0026rsquo;t have as many color options as paint, and they don\u0026rsquo;t have the smoothness paint\u0026rsquo;s consistency offers.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGlazed Cabinets\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eGlaze is applied over stains or paints to add more dimension and contrast to cabinets, particularly with shaker and raised-panel style doors. Where stains seep into the surface, glaze sits on top, with two different application methods that each have different effects.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThe first method is an accent glaze, which applies the glaze in corners and lines to create decorative contrast, like with our \u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/page/cabinets-white-wilora-hawthorne-shaker-antique-base/?utm_source=blog\u0026amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide\"\u003eantique white \u003c/a\u003ecollection. It\u0026rsquo;s used to highlight details in the cabinets without affecting the overall look. The second method is to add texture to the overall look of paints or stains.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOverall: Choose the Option You Love\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eSince paints and stains have such different qualities, it\u0026rsquo;s best to choose the style you like over the style you think others like. Go with the perfectly smooth finish of paint or embrace the natural features stains enhance. We offer both types so you can find the best fit for your home.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003eWhich Cabinet Design Style Matches Your Vision?\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eWith so many interior design styles out there, our Wilora Hawthorne and Wilora Paloma cabinets were designed to fit under the following styles: farmhouse, modern, classic, transitional, industrial, and cottage. Preassembled cabinets require little work, as you simply mount the boxes and install the doors, but they have the highest risk of damage during the shipping process. \u0026nbsp;RTA cabinets have the least risk of damage during shipping and are more affordable overall. \u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eFor RTA cabinets, you have a couple options when assembling and installing your cabinets. Hardware adds the final punctuation to the statement your cabinets make.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/catalog/hardware-cabinet-pulls/?utm_source=blog\u0026amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide\"\u003ePulls\u003c/a\u003e tend to be longer and bigger than knobs. Since your hand wraps around the pull, it provides greater leverage for opening and closing, making it ideal for drawers with heavy items and large doors. Lengths vary from around 1\u0026rdquo; to over 30\u0026rdquo;, meaning you have plenty of options for your cabinets, drawers and appliances. Consider the projection measurements, which tells you how far the pull protrudes from the cabinet. A longer projection allows for bigger hands and saves your knuckles from rubbing against cabinets. Projections range between \u0026frac12;\u0026quot; to 2\u0026rdquo;. Popular shapes include cup handles, bar pulls, rectangular, and curved.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/catalog/hardware-cabinet-knobs/?utm_source=blog\u0026amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide\"\u003eKnobs\u003c/a\u003e are smaller and designed for fingertips rather than palms. \u0026nbsp;Shapes for knobs consist of square, rectangular, round, simple, detailed, beveled, artisanal, and even translucent styles. are several \u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/resource-center/cabinet-materials/\" target=\"_blank\"\u003ecommon cabinet materials\u003c/a\u003e you can use: particle board, medium density fiberboard (MDF), high density fiberboard (HDF), and plywood. All are forms of engineered wood, but their density and stability are different.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cul\u003e\n\t\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eParticle Board: \u003c/strong\u003eMade from small wood particles fused together with resin. This is the least dense and durable, but the most affordable. It\u0026rsquo;s used primarily as an affordable option for cabinet boxes, but it tends to sag and buckle under heavy weights.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/li\u003e\n\t\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePlywood:\u003c/strong\u003e Thinly sliced layers of wood are bonded together with resin and high-pressure. This is the strongest of the four, making it the best choice to use in cabinet boxes and frames.\u003c/li\u003e\n\t\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMDF:\u003c/strong\u003e Made from wood fibers instead of particles, MDF uses resins and high pressure to bond everything together. Works best for shelves and doors since it isn\u0026rsquo;t as susceptible to warping as wood is.\u003c/li\u003e\n\t\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eHDF:\u003c/strong\u003e Similar to MDF but denser and stronger. Works well for shelves or doors. HDF is also much more resistant to warping than wood, which is why it works so well for doors.\u003c/li\u003e\n\t\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSolid Wood: \u003c/strong\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/resource-center/wood-kitchen-cabinet-types/\" target=\"_blank\"\u003eWood cabinets\u003c/a\u003e features a beautiful wood grain that offers a natural look to any room. Because it is completely natural, it is susceptible to expanding and contracting over time. However, it\u0026rsquo;s also a long-lasting material as well.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eAll the Wilora cabinet boxes we sell are made from either \u0026frac12;\u0026rdquo; or \u0026frac34;\u0026rdquo; thick plywood for a more durable construction than is found with particle board.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch3\u003eFramed vs Frameless\u003c/h3\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eBoth framed and frameless cabinet styles each have their pros and cons. It all comes down to your personal preference.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFramed\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThese cabinets feature a frame installed to the front of the cabinet box. The drawers and doors are connected to the frame instead of the cabinet box. This frame serves as both a function and a style, as it adds durability and rigidity to the cabinet box \u0026nbsp;while providing a classic look when you open a cabinet door.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThe main drawback with framed cabinets is access. \u0026nbsp;Since the frame is 1\u0026rdquo; to 2\u0026rdquo; wider than the thickness of the cabinet box, the frame can get in the way when storing or retrieving things like pots, pans, or spices.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eWith our framed selection of Wilora Hawthorne cabinets, the box interiors and exteriors are also given a UV coating to add protection to the natural Wood veneer finish.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFrameless\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThe doors of a frameless cabinet attach directly to the cabinet box, so there\u0026rsquo;s no need for a front frame. Generally, a frameless cabinet is easier to utilize and access. On the other hand, it weakens the cabinet box, especially if you use subpar materials. This is why a frameless cabinet box needs to be thicker than a cabinet box used on a framed style.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eFor this reason, our \u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/search/?q=wilora%20paloma\u0026amp;utm_source=blog\u0026amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide\"\u003eWilora Paloma\u003c/a\u003e selection of frameless cabinets feature \u0026frac34;\u0026rdquo; plywood boards in the construction of the cabinet boxes. The additional thickness provides the rigid stability necessary for holding doors and drawers. The Paloma collection also features European style flat-slab doors and drawers rather than the five-piece designs of our framed cabinet doors.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch3\u003eWhat\u0026rsquo;s a Door Overlay? Why It Matters?\u003c/h3\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eWith framed cabinets, a door overlay refers to the exposed front frame.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cul\u003e\n\t\u003cli\u003eWith a \u003cstrong\u003efull overlay\u003c/strong\u003e, most of the frame is covered by the doors and drawers.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/li\u003e\n\t\u003cli\u003eWith \u003cstrong\u003epartial overlay\u003c/strong\u003e, part of the frame is exposed.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/li\u003e\n\t\u003cli\u003eAn \u003cstrong\u003einset overlay\u003c/strong\u003e occurs when the door is flush with the frame.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eOur selection of cabinets offers full overlay for a more beautiful appearance.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003eWhich Cabinet Door Type Do You Like Best?\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThe door drives the style of your cabinets because this is what people see when they enter a room. With that in mind, there are three main styles of cabinet door and drawer: slab, shaker, and raised panel. There are other types, such as mullion and open-frame doors, but these are used sparingly. Most drawer and door designs fall into one of these three types. There\u0026rsquo;s arguably no difference in quality of the different styles. The differences are purely aesthetic, so choose one that you But style means little if it\u0026rsquo;s not functional. As you shop for the right cabinets for your home, there are some features to look for to optimize the functionality. Quality features help to extend the life of cabinetry and make your life easier (and quieter).\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eDrawer Slides\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/catalog/hardware-cabinets/?utm_source=blog\u0026amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide\"\u003eDrawer slides\u003c/a\u003e are located on the sides or under the drawer to help it move back and forth. Slides can either be install on the sides of the drawer, or underneath (called an under-mount slide). Premium cabinets use soft-close mechanism built into the slide so drawers don\u0026rsquo;t slam as they shut. Even if you try to slam a drawer, the soft-close feature slows \u0026nbsp;down to a smooth, soft stop.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eAnother feature to look for is whether the slides are full extension or not. Full extension means the drawer can be fully extended to see everything within the drawer. A \u0026frac34; extension glide leaves \u0026frac14; of the drawer inaccessible, making it harder to access items in the back of the drawer. That\u0026rsquo;s why full extension matters. It\u0026rsquo;s a small thing, but it affects your drawer organization later.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eOur framed cabinets feature Blum undermount, full extension soft-close drawer slides, so the hardware stay out of sight yet remains functional.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eOur frameless cabinets feature Blum\u0026rsquo;s \u0026ldquo;LegraBox\u0026rdquo; technology for a full extension, soft-close drawer as well.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eHinges\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eEven cabinet hinges are an indicator of quality. Much like drawers and drawer slides, a high-quality cabinet has soft-close hinges. These hinges prevent slamming doors, which extends the life of your cabinet boxes and doors alike. Quality hinges also make it easy to remove and re-attach doors for cleaning, painting, or organizing.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eKnown for their excellence in crafting quality cabinet hardware and accessories, Blum is a premium brand of hinges (and drawer slides). All our Wilora Paloma and Wilora Hawthorne cabinets come with soft-close Blum hardware. No upgrades required.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBumpers\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eA sign of a quality cabinet is if there are soft bumpers made of rubber on the inside corner of the cabinet door or drawer. These little pieces minimize the loud thud associated with shutting a door a bit too roughly. Over time, these may need to be replaced over the life of your cabinets, which is easy to do, especially if you choose the self-adhesive kind.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003eHow to Find the Perfect Cabinet contrasting well with light countertops, walls, and \u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/catalog/flooring/?utm_source=blog\u0026amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide\"\u003eflooring\u003c/a\u003e. The deep tones accentuate the silver metals, making the shine pop.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eDark cabinets add polish and depth, making them an ideal match for traditional or modern styles.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003eTantalizing Two-Tone Cabinets\u0026nbsp;\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eA practice that\u0026rsquo;s quickly catching on is using two colors of cabinets. There are a couple ways to do this to make sure colors work well in tandem.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThe most common method is to choose one color for the base cabinets and one for the wall cabinets. A general rule is to keep the base cabinets a darker color than the wall cabinets. Placing the darker color, such as dark grey, on the floor anchors the room, while the lighter color, perhaps a light grey, opens it up to create balance between the two.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eAnother method is to choose a color for the kitchen island while the base, wall, and tall cabinets are a different color or shade. This provides an additional pop of dimension to the room, preventing it from potentially looking flat.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003eCabinet Finish: Paint, Stain, or Glaze\u0026nbsp;\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThere are three options for cabinet finishes: paint, stain, or glaze. Each one has different properties and strengths that affect the longevity and appearance of your cabinets. The look also depends on the material of your cabinet doors. MDF and HDF don\u0026rsquo;t have wood grain, so they can\u0026rsquo;t be stained like solid wood.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePainted Cabinets\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003ePainted cabinets feature an \u0026nbsp;even coat, providing an opaque layer of solid color, hiding any wood grains or defining markings. Because of its smooth, pure appearance, it works best on MDF or HDF doors. On wood doors, paint hides the wood grain below, which may be a positive or negative depending on how you feel about wood grain.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003ePaint is the best choice for a flawlessly smooth color and surface. The main drawback to paint is tends to peel and crack over time, so take that into consideration as you think about what\u0026rsquo;s best for your home.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eStained Cabinets\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eStains are a translucent coating meant to enhance the grain and natural features of wood. Where paint covers, stains seep into the grain itself, darkening features like grains and knots while adding rich color tones.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eSince it\u0026rsquo;s translucent, stains are really only used with natural wood doors and cabinets instead of MDF or HDF materials, as these lack the natural grain stains are meant to enhance.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eStained cabinets tend to be easier to maintain over time and last longer because it doesn\u0026rsquo;t peel or crack. But stains don\u0026rsquo;t have as many color options as paint, and they don\u0026rsquo;t have the smoothness paint\u0026rsquo;s consistency offers.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGlazed Cabinets\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eGlaze is applied over stains or paints to add more dimension and contrast to cabinets, particularly with shaker and raised-panel style doors. Where stains seep into the surface, glaze sits on top, with two different application methods that each have different effects.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThe first method is an accent glaze, which applies the glaze in corners and lines to create decorative contrast, like with our \u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/page/cabinets-white-wilora-hawthorne-shaker-antique-base/?utm_source=blog\u0026amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide\"\u003eantique white \u003c/a\u003ecollection. It\u0026rsquo;s used to highlight details in the cabinets without affecting the overall look. The second method is to add texture to the overall look of paints or stains.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOverall: Choose the Option You Love\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eSince paints and stains have such different qualities, it\u0026rsquo;s best to choose the style you like over the style you think others like. Go with the perfectly smooth finish of paint or embrace the natural features stains enhance. We offer both types so you can find the best fit for your home.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003eWhich Cabinet Design Style Matches Your Vision?\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eWith so many interior design styles out there, our Wilora Hawthorne and Wilora Paloma cabinets were designed to fit under the following styles: farmhouse, modern, classic, transitional, industrial, and cottage. hardware includes pulls, knobs, and latches. Think of them like a watch on your wrist \u0026ndash; functional yet beautiful. Hardware adds the final punctuation to the statement your cabinets make.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/catalog/hardware-cabinet-pulls/?utm_source=blog\u0026amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide\"\u003ePulls\u003c/a\u003e tend to be longer and bigger than knobs. Since your hand wraps around the pull, it provides greater leverage for opening and closing, making it ideal for drawers with heavy items and large doors. Lengths vary from around 1\u0026rdquo; to over 30\u0026rdquo;, meaning you have plenty of options for your cabinets, drawers and appliances. Consider the projection measurements, which tells you how far the pull protrudes from the cabinet. A longer projection allows for bigger hands and saves your knuckles from rubbing against cabinets. Projections range between \u0026frac12;\u0026quot; to 2\u0026rdquo;. Popular shapes include cup handles, bar pulls, rectangular, and curved.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/catalog/hardware-cabinet-knobs/?utm_source=blog\u0026amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide\"\u003eKnobs\u003c/a\u003e are smaller and designed for fingertips rather than palms. \u0026nbsp;Shapes for knobs consist of square, rectangular, round, simple, detailed, beveled, artisanal, and even translucent styles. Knobs have projections ranging from \u0026frac12;\u0026quot; to 1 \u0026frac34;\u0026quot;, though it\u0026rsquo;s not as important as a pull\u0026rsquo;s projections.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://vevano.com/catalog/hardware-cabinets/?utm_source=blog\u0026amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20guide\"\u003eLatches\u003c/a\u003e are a quick way to secure loose doors while adding a rustic touch. They\u0026rsquo;re perfect for cottage and farmhouse kitchens. Latch styles range from simple to ornate, with materials like solid brass, stainless steel, nickel, gold, chrome, bronze, antiqued finishes, transparent acrylic, and matte black.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003ch2\u003eHow to Update Kitchen Cabinets Without Replacing Them\u003c/h2\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eIf new cabinets aren\u0026rsquo;t a feasible option yet, you can take some steps to revitalize and extend the life of your current cabinets.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eReplace or Add Parts\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eAs glides and hinges get older, smooth motions becomes squeaky, rough, or parts may break altogether. Upgrade old hinges and slides with new versions to restore effortless motion and operation. Try a completely different design style for a new aesthetic.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eOlder cabinets often don\u0026rsquo;t stay closed when you shut them.
